**Findings**
- **FIX:** Device-to-sender WS messages are not forwarded to the webhook. The current `message` branch only sends an ack, and the comment still says “webhook forwarding is step 5” ([server/app/routers/live.py](D:/Projects/syncler/server/app/routers/live.py:614)). This is not just incomplete coverage; it breaks the promised wire contract for `live_inbound_url`.
- **FIX:** Android uses `plugin.manifest.id` as `pluginRowId` ([PluginLoader.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/plugin-host/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/android/pluginhost/PluginLoader.kt:224)), but the server WS path expects a UUID plugin row id. `PluginManifest.id` is the manifest/plugin identifier shape ([PluginManifest.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/plugin-host/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/android/pluginhost/PluginManifest.kt:6)). Once `no_session` is wired, live connect likely fails as malformed `plugin_row_id`.
- **FIX:** `LiveBridge.send()` and `close()` call `clientChannelHandle()`, which calls `openChannel()` ([LiveBridge.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/plugin-host/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/android/pluginhost/capabilities/LiveBridge.kt:174)). That means `send()` on an unopened channel can silently open it, contradicting the `channel_not_open` contract. Also, repeated `connect()` calls re-run `wireIncoming()` and can attach duplicate collectors.
- **FIX:** `LiveBridge.closeForPlugin()` exists but is not called from crash/unload lifecycle paths ([LiveBridge.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/plugin-host/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/android/pluginhost/capabilities/LiveBridge.kt:118), [PluginLoader.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/plugin-host/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/android/pluginhost/PluginLoader.kt:417)). Plugin unload can leave a WS client and reconnect loop alive.

**Concern Verdicts**
1. **OK:** Subprotocol parsing is fine for `syncler.v1, bearer.<token>`; comma split plus trim handles ordinary whitespace/reordering. Echoing only `syncler.v1` is correct.
2. **OK for v0.1:** In async FastAPI single-process posture, no `await` occurs inside mint/redeem mutation. GIL plus event-loop serialization is enough. Redis swap remains required for multi-worker.
3. **NIT:** Fail-open revocation publish is acceptable, but log it. The comment mentions heartbeat re-check, but only pong timeout exists.
4. **NIT:** Per-socket rate limit is acceptable for v0.1, but document it as such. “Per plugin” should become a shared bucket before production.
5. **OK:** Any inbound frame extending liveness is a defensible lenient heartbeat policy.
6. **FIX:** Webhook signing fail-open is too quiet. If a webhook URL is configured and no signing seed exists, either refuse forwarding or make this debug-only with loud audit/logging.
7. **NIT:** Bus-only is acceptable for v0.1, but add polling before Redis swap or as part of it. Silent control-plane loss is otherwise long-lived auth drift.
8. **NIT:** The `no_session` placeholder is honest, but make it louder via audit/Timber because otherwise live appears “implemented” while always failing.
9. **NIT:** Add a local closed flag. Idempotent close is fine, but post-close `send()` should fail locally with `channel_not_open`, not wait for server error.
10. **FIX:** Add client-side 64 KB frame/envelope cap before base64/send ([LiveChannelClient.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/plugin-host/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/android/pluginhost/live/LiveChannelClient.kt:99)).
11. **DESIGN:** 256 replay entries is okay only if loss is explicit. Add a replay-gap signal or documented “best effort, may truncate” contract.
12. **NIT now, FIX before prod:** Accept dev HTTP, but validate `live_inbound_url` with the same scheme/host policy used for action endpoints.
13. **FIX before greenlight:** Given the webhook path is not actually wired and WS tests are smoke-only, I would not start V3 #16 yet. Add at least server e2e for message→webhook ack/error, revocation close, rate-limit close, and push fan-out once PG is back.

**Greenlight**
Not green for V3 #16 yet. Minimal pre-V3 #16 fix list: wire webhook forwarding, fix Android plugin row id source, prevent send/close from opening channels, close live clients on unload/crash, add client frame cap, and add the missing WS e2e tests.

That means `send()` on an unopened channel can silently open it, contradicting the `channel_not_open` contract. Also, repeated `connect()` calls re-run `wireIncoming()` and can attach duplicate collectors.
- **FIX:** `LiveBridge.closeForPlugin()` exists but is not called from crash/unload lifecycle paths ([LiveBridge.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/plugin-host/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/android/pluginhost/capabilities/LiveBridge.kt:118), [PluginLoader.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/plugin-host/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/android/pluginhost/PluginLoader.kt:417)). Plugin unload can leave a WS client and reconnect loop alive.

**Concern Verdicts**
1. **OK:** Subprotocol parsing is fine for `syncler.v1, bearer.<token>`; comma split plus trim handles ordinary whitespace/reordering. Echoing only `syncler.v1` is correct.
2. **OK for v0.1:** In async FastAPI single-process posture, no `await` occurs inside mint/redeem mutation. GIL plus event-loop serialization is enough. Redis swap remains required for multi-worker.
3. **NIT:** Fail-open revocation publish is acceptable, but log it. The comment mentions heartbeat re-check, but only pong timeout exists.
4. **NIT:** Per-socket rate limit is acceptable for v0.1, but document it as such. “Per plugin” should become a shared bucket before production.
5. **OK:** Any inbound frame extending liveness is a defensible lenient heartbeat policy.
6. **FIX:** Webhook signing fail-open is too quiet. If a webhook URL is configured and no signing seed exists, either refuse forwarding or make this debug-only with loud audit/logging.
7. **NIT:** Bus-only is acceptable for v0.1, but add polling before Redis swap or as part of it. Silent control-plane loss is otherwise long-lived auth drift.
8. **NIT:** The `no_session` placeholder is honest, but make it louder via audit/Timber because otherwise live appears “implemented” while always failing.
9. **NIT:** Add a local closed flag. Idempotent close is fine, but post-close `send()` should fail locally with `channel_not_open`, not wait for server error.
10. **FIX:** Add client-side 64 KB frame/envelope cap before base64/send ([LiveChannelClient.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/plugin-host/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/android/pluginhost/live/LiveChannelClient.kt:99)).
11. **DESIGN:** 256 replay entries is okay only if loss is explicit. Add a replay-gap signal or documented “best effort, may truncate” contract.
12. **NIT now, FIX before prod:** Accept dev HTTP, but validate `live_inbound_url` with the same scheme/host policy used for action endpoints.
13. **FIX before greenlight:** Given the webhook path is not actually wired and WS tests are smoke-only, I would not start V3 #16 yet. Add at least server e2e for message→webhook ack/error, revocation close, rate-limit close, and push fan-out once PG is back.

**Greenlight**
Not green for V3 #16 yet. Minimal pre-V3 #16 fix list: wire webhook forwarding, fix Android plugin row id source, prevent send/close from opening channels, close live clients on unload/crash, add client frame cap, and add the missing WS e2e tests.
